***konijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:konijn.html>konijn</a> (2931)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">conijn</i>, from earlier Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">conin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">connin</i>, a variant of Old French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">conil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cuniculus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύνικλος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúniklos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iberian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Iberian language">Iberian</a></span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celtiberian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Celtiberian language">Celtiberian</a></span> origin. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cony</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kaninchen</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">conejo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rabbit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:konijn.html>konijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:konijnen.html>konijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:konijntje.html>konijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">rabbit</span>, a bunny; any non-hare lagomorph of the family Leporidae.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">rob</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">konijnenbout</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:konijnenhok.html>konijnenhok</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:konijnenhol.html>konijnenhol</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">konijnenjacht</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">konijnenpoot</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">stresskonijn</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***kont.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kont.html>kont</a> (1012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">conte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vagina”, also generally “sex organ</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:kunta.html>kunta</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:vagina.html>vagina</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kuntǭ</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cunt.html>cunt</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kont.html>kont</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:konten.html>konten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kontje.html>kontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> butt, bum, <a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a <a href = vnd.unilang:cunt.html>cunt</a> (an extremely unpleasant or objectionable person)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:cunt.html>cunt</a>, female genitalia</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The Middle Dutch sense of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cunt.html>cunt</a></i> (“female genitalia”) <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> disappeared almost entirely from modern Dutch, save for dialects of Flanders, Groningen, and Friesland; this sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> entirely absent in general speech. The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not particularly vulgar, being perhaps more equivalent to “butt” than “arse, ass”.</li>
<li>Among younger <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kont.html>kont</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> on the meaning of “an extremely unpleasant or objectionable person”, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> likely due to the influence of British English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cunt.html>cunt</a></i> with the more vulgar sense.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bofkont</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kontlikker.html>kontlikker</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kont.html>kont</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:informeel.html>informeel</a>)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(dierkunde)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:billen.html>billen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterwerk.html>achterwerk</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> z'n <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kont.html>kont</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a>.</i> </li>
<li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>Maar</a> Albert <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vlug.html>vlug</a> type, <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kostte.html>kostte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a>. <a ***kool.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kool.html>kool</a> (8234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">col</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:cole.html>cole</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kōl</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kōla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caulis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kool.html>kool</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kolen.html>kolen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kooltje.html>kooltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cabbage</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:cole.html>cole</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:kol.html>kol</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kolo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kulą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷol-</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǴwelH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to burn, shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. May originate from a neuter plurale tantum that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> reanalysed as a feminine singular; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:kol.html>kol</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">koal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kohle</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">coal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:kul.html>kul</a></i>.
</p>

***koord.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koord.html>koord</a> (13730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">corde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">coorde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">corde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">chorda</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> (Doric) <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χορδά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khordá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Ionic <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χορδή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khordḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">string of gut, the string of a lyre</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublette with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">koorde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straight line connecting two dots of a curve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***koorts.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koorts.html>koorts</a> (3548)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">corts</i>, further etymology unknown, with apparently no direct Germanic language cognates.  An indirect relationship with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kool.html>kool</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> suggested, <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǴwelH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burn, shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="skt">ज्वलति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burn brightly, blaze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="skt">ज्वर</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fever, pain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  But this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> quite speculative as all Germanic derivatives of this root have the sense of <i>coal.</i>
</p>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koortsachtig.html>koortsachtig</a> (56970)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koorts.html>koorts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-achtig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ly, -ish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koortsachtig.html>koortsachtig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koortsachtig.html>koortsachtiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">koortsachtigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> feverous, suffering from fever</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (by far the most common use) frenetic, feverish, nervous, haste-stressed</li>
<li>resembling fever</li>
<li>causing fever</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***kop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a> (430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cop</i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cuppa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koppen.html>koppen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kopje.html>kopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cup (for drinking)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>Nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kopje.html>kopje</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">(Do you want) another <b>cup</b> of tea?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mok.html>mok</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">for animals<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial and derogatory  for humans</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> head
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Buldogs <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:angstaanjagend.html>angstaanjagende</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:bulldogs.html>Bulldogs</a> have a scary <b>head</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>Hou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Shut your hole!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A (male) human.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwaaie.html>kwaaie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What an angry <b>guy</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>head of a nail, pin etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slaat.html>slaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spijker.html>spijker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You hit the nail on the <b>head</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>front, lead, e.g. in a race; charge, control.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:underdog.html>underdog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:underdog.html>underdog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in the <b>lead</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>heading <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a text</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, headline</li>
<li>heads <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">side of a coin</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruis.html>kruis</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:munt.html>munt</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>pegbox (part of a stringed instrument that holds the tuning pegs)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered impolite to refer to someone's head with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></i>. That word normally only refers to the head of animals, although for <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a>, which are considered noble animals, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally used.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***kopen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kopen.html>kopen</a> (636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">côpen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">cōpon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kaupōną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caupō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kopen.html>kopen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to buy

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>Hebben</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gekocht.html>gekocht</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <b>buy</b> too much?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***koper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koper.html>koper</a> (5154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">coper</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cuprum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koper.html>koper</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>copper <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">metal, element</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kopen.html>kopen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koperen.html>koperen</a> (14942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koper.html>koper</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i> 'copper', from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koperen.html>koperen</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>(consisting of) copper, coppern</li>
<li>(made of) brass, brazen</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kopererts</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">koperkleur</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">verkoperen</span> (verb)</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href = vnd.unilang:koper.html>koper</a> 'copper' (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span>) + verbal ending -en
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koperen.html>koperen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To copper, mount, cover, coat or otherwise fit with copper or brassware</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To copper, colour (e.g. paint) like brass</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To have the colour of brass</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koraal.html>koraal</a> (26615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">corael</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">coral</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corallium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κοραλλιών</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koralliṓn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">coral</i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koraal.html>koraal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koralen.html>koralen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koraal.html>koraaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A coral; any of various coralline tiny organisms of the class Anthozoa, notably of genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Corallium" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Corallium"><i>Corallium</i></a></span>, who live in marine colonies.</li>
<li>The coral (calceous substance) they produce while building their colonies.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">organism</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">koraaldier</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">koraalpoliep</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">koraalbank</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">koraaleiland</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">koraalmos</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koraalrif.html>koraalrif</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">koraalrood</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">koraalslang</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">Koraalzee</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koralen.html>koralen</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">koralijn</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koraal.html>koraal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koralen.html>koralen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koraal.html>koraaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A bead made from or resembling natural coral.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">choralis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koraal.html>koraal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koralen.html>koralen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koraal.html>koraaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A male chorister, choir singer, choir boy (especially a treble).</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">koorzanger</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koorknaap.html>koorknaap</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koraal.html>koraal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koralen.html>koralen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koraal.html>koraaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A chorale, religious musical genre.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_3">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">koraalgezang</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***kordon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kordon.html>kordon</a> (47075)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:koren.html>koren</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">corn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">korn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">coren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kurną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵr̥h₂nóm</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Koorn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Korn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">corn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">korn</i>.Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graan.html>graan</a></i>.

***kornuit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kornuit.html>kornuit</a> (104138)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cornuut</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cornut</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cornūtus</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">corps</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corpus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">body</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷrép-o-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*Kʷr̥p-eH₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">body</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
